						<article id="post-386875" class="post-386875 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail  category-clima tag-ciclone tag-frente-fria tag-previsao tag-regiao-sul tag-destaque-primeira-pagina single-post-content has-thumbnail">

								<nav role="navigation" aria-label="Breadcrumbs" class="bf-breadcrumb clearfix bc-align-center"><ul class="bf-breadcrumb-items" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/BreadcrumbList"><meta name="numberOfItems" content="3"><meta name="itemListOrder" content="Ascending"><li itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" class="bf-breadcrumb-item bf-breadcrumb-begin"><a itemprop="item" href="https://portallitoralsul.com.br" rel="home"><span itemprop="name">Início</span></a><meta itemprop="position" content="1"></li><li itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" class="bf-breadcrumb-item"><a itemprop="item" href="https://portallitoralsul.com.br/categoria/clima/"><span itemprop="name">Clima</span></a><meta itemprop="position" content="2"></li><li itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" class="bf-breadcrumb-item bf-breadcrumb-end"><span itemprop="name">Ciclone e frente fria se aproximam da Região Sul; veja previsão</span><meta itemprop="item" content="https://portallitoralsul.com.br/ciclone-e-frente-fria-se-aproximam-da-regiao-sul-veja-previsao/"><meta itemprop="position" content="3"></li></ul></nav><div class="term-badges floated"><span class="term-badge term-18769"><a href="https://portallitoralsul.com.br/categoria/clima/">Clima</a></span></div>									<h1 class="single-post-title">
										<span class="post-title" itemprop="headline">Ciclone e frente fria se aproximam da Região Sul; veja previsão</span></h1>
									<h2 class="post-subtitle">Na quinta-feira, dia 2, previsão é que ocorra temporais </h2>									<div class="post-meta-wrap clearfix">
										<div class="post-meta single-post-meta">
			<a href="https://portallitoralsul.com.br/author/comercialportallitoralsul-com-br/" title="Artigos de autor" class="post-author-a post-author-avatar">
			<span class="post-author-name">De <b>Redação</b></span>		</a>
					<span class="time"><time class="post-published updated" datetime="2023-10-31T08:07:17-03:00">Em <b>31 out, 2023 | 08:07</b></time></span>
			</div>
									</div>

									<a class="post-thumbnail open-lightbox" href="https://portallitoralsul.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/IMG_2879-e1665484297847.jpg"><img width="1130" height="580" alt="" data-src="https://portallitoralsul.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/IMG_2879-1130x580.jpg"></a>											<span class="image-credit">Foto: Caroline Sartori/Portal Litoral Sul</span>

														<div class="entry-content clearfix single-post-content">
								<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A </span><b>terça-feira, dia 31, </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">amanheceu com uma garoa, que deve seguir durante todo o período no Litoral Sul. Entre a tarde e à noite em todas as regiões há condições para pancadas isoladas de chuva e trovoadas que intercalam com períodos de melhora, por influência de </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">oscilações</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> em diversos níveis da atmosfera e do fluxo de calor e umidade vindo do Norte do país. A temperatura mínima&nbsp; varia entre 17 e 21°C. As máximas variam entre 13 e 20°C nos planaltos e no Litoral Sul. Ao longo da noite, pode ocorrer rajadas fracas de vento pelo estado.</span></p><div class="ai-viewports ai-viewport-3 ai-insert-39-36686241" style="margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;" data-insertion-position="prepend" data-selector=".ai-insert-39-36686241" data-insertion-no-dbg="" data-code="PGRpdiBjbGFzcz0nY29kZS1ibG9jayBjb2RlLWJsb2NrLWNlbnRlciBjb2RlLWJsb2NrLTM5IGFpLXRyYWNrJyBkYXRhLWFpPSdXek01TENJaUxDSlhhR0YwYzBGd2NDQXRJRWx1ZEdWeWJtOGdLRTF2WW1sc1pTa2lMQ0lpTERGZCc+Cgo8c3R5bGU+Ci5haS1yb3RhdGUge3Bvc2l0aW9uOiByZWxhdGl2ZTt9Ci5haS1yb3RhdGUtaGlkZGVuIHt2aXNpYmlsaXR5OiBoaWRkZW47fQouYWktcm90YXRlLWhpZGRlbi0yIHtwb3NpdGlvbjogYWJzb2x1dGU7IHRvcDogMDsgbGVmdDogMDsgd2lkdGg6IDEwMCU7IGhlaWdodDogMTAwJTt9Ci5haS1saXN0LWRhdGEsIC5haS1pcC1kYXRhLCAuYWktZmlsdGVyLWNoZWNrLCAuYWktZmFsbGJhY2ssIC5haS1saXN0LWJsb2NrLCAuYWktbGlzdC1ibG9jay1pcCwgLmFpLWxpc3QtYmxvY2stZmlsdGVyIHt2aXNpYmlsaXR5OiBoaWRkZW47IHBvc2l0aW9uOiBhYnNvbHV0ZTsgd2lkdGg6IDUwJTsgaGVpZ2h0OiAxcHg7IHRvcDogLTEwMDBweDsgei1pbmRleDogLTk5OTk7IG1hcmdpbjogMHB4IWltcG9ydGFudDt9Ci5haS1saXN0LWRhdGEsIC5haS1pcC1kYXRhLCAuYWktZmlsdGVyLWNoZWNrLCAuYWktZmFsbGJhY2sge21pbi13aWR0aDogMXB4O30KPC9zdHlsZT4KPGRpdiBjbGFzcz0nYWktcm90YXRlIGFpLXVucHJvY2Vzc2VkIGFpLXRpbWVkLXJvdGF0aW9uIGFpLTM5LTEnIGRhdGEtaW5mbz0nV3lJek9TMHhJaXd4WFE9PSc+CjxkaXYgY2xhc3M9J2FpLXJvdGF0ZS1vcHRpb24gYWktcm90YXRlLWhpZGRlbicgZGF0YS1pbmRleD0iMSIgZGF0YS1uYW1lPSJSM0oxY0c4Z01RPT0iIGRhdGEtdGltZT0iT0E9PSI+CjxhIGhyZWY9Imh0dHBzOi8vY2hhdC53aGF0c2FwcC5jb20vRnBhdzVNS0JVZzJCOUFYV2hhTDJqNiI+PGltZyBzcmM9Imh0dHBzOi8vcG9ydGFsbGl0b3JhbHN1bC5jb20uYnIvd3AtY29udGVudC91cGxvYWRzLzIwMjMvMDcvYmFubmVyLXdoYXRzYXBwLW1vYmlsZS5qcGciPjwvYT48L2Rpdj4KPC9kaXY+CjwvZGl2Pgo=" data-block="39"></div>

<div class="ai-viewports ai-viewport-2 ai-insert-38-77338556" style="margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;" data-insertion-position="prepend" data-selector=".ai-insert-38-77338556" data-insertion-no-dbg="" data-code="PGRpdiBjbGFzcz0nY29kZS1ibG9jayBjb2RlLWJsb2NrLWNlbnRlciBjb2RlLWJsb2NrLTM4IGFpLXRyYWNrJyBkYXRhLWFpPSdXek00TENJaUxDSlhhR0YwYzBGd2NDQXRJRWx1ZEdWeWJtOGdLRlJoWW14bGRDa2lMQ0lpTERGZCc+Cgo8c3R5bGU+Ci5haS1yb3RhdGUge3Bvc2l0aW9uOiByZWxhdGl2ZTt9Ci5haS1yb3RhdGUtaGlkZGVuIHt2aXNpYmlsaXR5OiBoaWRkZW47fQouYWktcm90YXRlLWhpZGRlbi0yIHtwb3NpdGlvbjogYWJzb2x1dGU7IHRvcDogMDsgbGVmdDogMDsgd2lkdGg6IDEwMCU7IGhlaWdodDogMTAwJTt9Ci5haS1saXN0LWRhdGEsIC5haS1pcC1kYXRhLCAuYWktZmlsdGVyLWNoZWNrLCAuYWktZmFsbGJhY2ssIC5haS1saXN0LWJsb2NrLCAuYWktbGlzdC1ibG9jay1pcCwgLmFpLWxpc3QtYmxvY2stZmlsdGVyIHt2aXNpYmlsaXR5OiBoaWRkZW47IHBvc2l0aW9uOiBhYnNvbHV0ZTsgd2lkdGg6IDUwJTsgaGVpZ2h0OiAxcHg7IHRvcDogLTEwMDBweDsgei1pbmRleDogLTk5OTk7IG1hcmdpbjogMHB4IWltcG9ydGFudDt9Ci5haS1saXN0LWRhdGEsIC5haS1pcC1kYXRhLCAuYWktZmlsdGVyLWNoZWNrLCAuYWktZmFsbGJhY2sge21pbi13aWR0aDogMXB4O30KPC9zdHlsZT4KPGRpdiBjbGFzcz0nYWktcm90YXRlIGFpLXVucHJvY2Vzc2VkIGFpLXRpbWVkLXJvdGF0aW9uIGFpLTM4LTEnIGRhdGEtaW5mbz0nV3lJek9DMHhJaXd4WFE9PSc+CjxkaXYgY2xhc3M9J2FpLXJvdGF0ZS1vcHRpb24gYWktcm90YXRlLWhpZGRlbicgZGF0YS1pbmRleD0iMSIgZGF0YS1uYW1lPSJSM0oxY0c4Z01RPT0iIGRhdGEtdGltZT0iT0E9PSI+CjxhIGhyZWY9Imh0dHBzOi8vY2hhdC53aGF0c2FwcC5jb20vRnBhdzVNS0JVZzJCOUFYV2hhTDJqNiI+PGltZyBzcmM9Imh0dHBzOi8vcG9ydGFsbGl0b3JhbHN1bC5jb20uYnIvd3AtY29udGVudC91cGxvYWRzLzIwMjMvMDcvYmFubmVyLXdoYXRzYXBwLXRhYmxldC5qcGciPjwvYT48L2Rpdj4KPC9kaXY+CjwvZGl2Pgo=" data-block="38"></div>

<div class="ai-viewports ai-viewport-1 ai-insert-37-18019546" style="margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;" data-insertion-position="prepend" data-selector=".ai-insert-37-18019546" data-insertion-no-dbg="" data-code="PGRpdiBjbGFzcz0nY29kZS1ibG9jayBjb2RlLWJsb2NrLWNlbnRlciBjb2RlLWJsb2NrLTM3IGFpLXRyYWNrJyBkYXRhLWFpPSdXek0zTENJaUxDSlhhR0YwYzBGd2NDQXRJRWx1ZEdWeWJtOGdLRVJsYzJ0MGIzQXBJaXdpSWl3eFhRPT0nPgoKPHN0eWxlPgouYWktcm90YXRlIHtwb3NpdGlvbjogcmVsYXRpdmU7fQouYWktcm90YXRlLWhpZGRlbiB7dmlzaWJpbGl0eTogaGlkZGVuO30KLmFpLXJvdGF0ZS1oaWRkZW4tMiB7cG9zaXRpb246IGFic29sdXRlOyB0b3A6IDA7IGxlZnQ6IDA7IHdpZHRoOiAxMDAlOyBoZWlnaHQ6IDEwMCU7fQouYWktbGlzdC1kYXRhLCAuYWktaXAtZGF0YSwgLmFpLWZpbHRlci1jaGVjaywgLmFpLWZhbGxiYWNrLCAuYWktbGlzdC1ibG9jaywgLmFpLWxpc3QtYmxvY2staXAsIC5haS1saXN0LWJsb2NrLWZpbHRlciB7dmlzaWJpbGl0eTogaGlkZGVuOyBwb3NpdGlvbjogYWJzb2x1dGU7IHdpZHRoOiA1MCU7IGhlaWdodDogMXB4OyB0b3A6IC0xMDAwcHg7IHotaW5kZXg6IC05OTk5OyBtYXJnaW46IDBweCFpbXBvcnRhbnQ7fQouYWktbGlzdC1kYXRhLCAuYWktaXAtZGF0YSwgLmFpLWZpbHRlci1jaGVjaywgLmFpLWZhbGxiYWNrIHttaW4td2lkdGg6IDFweDt9Cjwvc3R5bGU+CjxkaXYgY2xhc3M9J2FpLXJvdGF0ZSBhaS11bnByb2Nlc3NlZCBhaS10aW1lZC1yb3RhdGlvbiBhaS0zNy0xJyBkYXRhLWluZm89J1d5SXpOeTB4SWl3eFhRPT0nPgo8ZGl2IGNsYXNzPSdhaS1yb3RhdGUtb3B0aW9uIGFpLXJvdGF0ZS1oaWRkZW4nIGRhdGEtaW5kZXg9IjEiIGRhdGEtbmFtZT0iUjNKMWNHOGdNUT09IiBkYXRhLXRpbWU9Ik9BPT0iPgo8YSBocmVmPSJodHRwczovL2NoYXQud2hhdHNhcHAuY29tL0ZwYXc1TUtCVWcyQjlBWFdoYUwyajYiPjxpbWcgc3JjPSJodHRwczovL3BvcnRhbGxpdG9yYWxzdWwuY29tLmJyL3dwLWNvbnRlbnQvdXBsb2Fkcy8yMDIzLzA3L2Jhbm5lci1ub3ZvLXdoYXRzYXBwLWRlc2t0b3AuanBnIj48L2E+PC9kaXY+CjwvZGl2Pgo8L2Rpdj4K" data-block="37"></div>


<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A chuva fraca deve se manter nesta </span><b>quarta-feira, dia 1º, </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;devido a circulação marítima. As temperaturas mínimas variam entre 17 e 21°C na Região Sul. À tarde as máximas oscilam entre 13 e 20°C no Litoral Sul. Entre a tarde e à noite nas áreas costeiras, pode ocorrer rajadas moderadas.&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Esta condição deve seguir durante toda a semana. As instabilidades ganham reforço devido ao processo de formação de um ciclone extratropical associado à passagem de uma frente fria que avança em direção ao estado pelas áreas de divisa com o RS. A partir de quinta-feira, dia 2, pode ocorrer temporais com raios, rajadas de vento, eventual queda de granizo, alagamentos e risco de enxurradas.</span></p>
<p>Fonte: Defesa Civil</p>
